﻿# Misr Spinning and Weaving Company
company_misr = {
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/company_icons/historical_company_icons/misr.dds"
	background = "gfx/interface/icons/company_icons/company_backgrounds/comp_illu_manufacturing_light.dds"
	
	flavored_company = yes
	
	building_types = { 
		building_textile_mills
		building_cotton_plantation
	}
	
	potential = {
		has_interest_marker_in_region = region_nile_basin
	}	
	
	attainable = {
		hidden_trigger = { # Hide attainable if it's always fulfilled by possible
			any_scope_state = {
				state_region = s:STATE_LOWER_EGYPT
			}	
		}
	}
	
	possible = { 
		any_scope_state = {
			state_region = s:STATE_LOWER_EGYPT
			is_incorporated = yes
			any_scope_building = {
				is_building_type = building_textile_mills
				level >= 3
			}
		}
		has_technology_researched = corporate_charters
	}
	
	prosperity_modifier = {
		state_loyalists_from_sol_change_mult = 0.1
	}	
	
	ai_weight = {
		value = 3 # Higher base value for flavored companies
	}
}

# Egyptian National Railways
company_egyptian_rail = {
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/company_icons/historical_company_icons/egyptian_rail.dds"
	background = "gfx/interface/icons/company_icons/company_backgrounds/comp_illu_railways.dds"
	
	flavored_company = yes
	
	building_types = { 
		building_railway
	}
	
	potential = {
		country_has_primary_culture = cu:misri
	}		

	possible = { 
		any_scope_state = {
			region = sr:region_nile_basin
			is_incorporated = yes
			has_building = building_railway
			count >= 4
		}
		has_technology_researched = corporate_charters			
	}
	
	prosperity_modifier = {
		state_infrastructure_from_population_max_add = 20
		market_land_trade_capacity_add = 10
	}	
	
	ai_weight = {
		value = 3 # Higher base value for flavored companies
	}
}

			}

	possible = {

		country_tax_income_add = 50000

		value = 3 # Higher base value for flavored companies
	}
}

﻿# United Company of Merchants of England Trading to the East Indies
company_east_india_company = {
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/company_icons/historical_company_icons/gb_eic.dds"
	background = "gfx/interface/icons/company_icons/company_backgrounds/comp_illu_plantation.dds"
	
	flavored_company = yes
	
	building_types = {  
		building_tea_plantation
		building_tobacco_plantation
		building_opium_plantation
	}
	
	potential = {
		c:BIC ?= this
	}
	
	possible = {
		c:BIC ?= this
		any_scope_state = {
			OR = {
				region = sr:region_north_india
				region = sr:region_south_india
			}
			any_scope_building = {
				OR = {
					is_building_type = building_tea_plantation
					is_building_type = building_tobacco_plantation
					is_building_type = building_opium_plantation
				}
				level >= 3
			}
			count >= 4
		}
		OR = {
			has_law = law_type:law_mercantilism
			has_law = law_type:law_protectionism
		}
	}
	
	prosperity_modifier = {
		country_convoys_capacity_mult = 0.2
	}	
	
	ai_weight = {
		value = 3 # Higher base value for flavored companies
	}
}

# Great Indian Peninsula Railway
company_great_indian_railway = {
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/company_icons/historical_company_icons/india_great_indian_peninsula_railway.dds"

	building_types = {  
		building_railway
	}
	
	potential = {
		OR = {
			has_interest_marker_in_region = region_south_india
			has_interest_marker_in_region = region_north_india
		}
	}
	
	attainable = {
		hidden_trigger = { # Hide attainable if it's always fulfilled by possible
			any_scope_state = {
				OR = {
					region = sr:region_south_india
					region = sr:region_north_india
				}
			}
		}
	}			
	
	possible = {
		any_scope_state = {
			OR = {
				region = sr:region_south_india
				region = sr:region_north_india
			}

		building_paper_mills
		building_logging_camp
		building_power_plant
	}
	
	potential = {
		has_interest_marker_in_region = region_baltic
	}
	
	attainable = {
		hidden_trigger = { # Hide attainable if it's always fulfilled by possible
			any_scope_state = {
				state_region = s:STATE_UUSIMAA
			}
		}
	}		
	
	possible = {
		any_scope_state = {
			state_region = s:STATE_UUSIMAA
			is_incorporated = yes
			any_scope_building = {
				is_building_type = building_paper_mills
				level >= 3
			}
		}
		has_technology_researched = atmospheric_engine
	}
	
	prosperity_modifier = {
		building_electrics_industry_throughput_add = 0.1
		building_synthetics_plants_throughput_add = 0.05
	}	
	
	ai_weight = {
		value = 3 # Higher base value for flavored companies
	}
}

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/company_icons/historical_company_icons/german_krupp.dds"
	background = "gfx/interface/icons/company_icons/company_backgrounds/comp_illu_manufacturing_heavy.dds"
	
	flavored_company = yes
	
	building_types = {  
		building_arms_industry
		building_artillery_foundries
		building_steel_mills
	}
	
	potential = {
		has_interest_marker_in_region = region_north_germany
	}
	
	attainable = {
		hidden_trigger = { # Hide attainable if it's always fulfilled by possible
			any_scope_state = {
				state_region = s:STATE_RUHR
			}
		}
	}	
	
	possible = { 
		any_scope_state = {
			state_region = s:STATE_RUHR
			is_incorporated = yes
			any_scope_building = {
				OR = {
					is_building_type = building_steel_mills
					is_building_type = building_arms_industry
					is_building_type = building_artillery_foundries
				}
				level >= 3
			}
		}
		has_technology_researched = steelworking
	}
	
	prosperity_modifier = {
		building_railway_throughput_add = 0.1
		unit_kill_rate_add = 0.1
	}	
	
	ai_weight = {
		value = 3 # Higher base value for flavored companies
	}
}

# Rheinische Metallwaaren- und Maschinenfabrik Aktiengesellschaft
company_rheinmetall = {
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/company_icons/historical_company_icons/german_rheinmetall.dds"
	background = "gfx/interface/icons/company_icons/company_backgrounds/comp_illu_manufacturing_heavy.dds"
	
	flavored_company = yes
	
	building_types = {  
		building_artillery_foundries
		building_munition_plants
		building_explosives_factory
	}
	
	potential = {
		has_interest_marker_in_region = region_north_germany
	}
	
	attainable = {
		hidden_trigger = { # Hide attainable if it's always fulfilled by possible
			any_scope_state = {
				OR = {
					state_region = s:STATE_RUHR
					state_region = s:STATE_NORTH_RHINE
				}
			}
		}
	}		
	
	possible = {
		any_scope_state = {
			OR = {
				state_region = s:STATE_RUHR
				state_region = s:STATE_NORTH_RHINE
			}
			is_incorporated = yes
			any_scope_building = {
				OR = {
					is_building_type = building_arms_industry
					is_building_type = building_artillery_foundries
					is_building_type = building_munition_plants
				}
				level >= 3
			}
		}
		has_technology_researched = automatic_machine_guns
	}
	
	prosperity_modifier = {
		unit_combat_unit_type_siege_artillery_offense_mult = 0.1
		unit_combat_unit_type_shrapnel_artillery_offense_mult = 0.1
		unit_army_defense_mult = 0.05
	}

	ai_weight = {
		value = 3 # Higher base value for flavored companies
	}	
}

# Preußische Staatseisenbahnen
company_prussian_state_railways = {
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/company_icons/historical_company_icons/german_kpev.dds"
	background = "gfx/interface/icons/company_icons/company_backgrounds/comp_illu_railways.dds"
	
	flavored_company = yes
	
	building_types = {  
		building_railway
	}
	
	potential = {
		OR = {
			c:PRU ?= this
			was_formed_from = PRU
		}
	}
	
	possible = {
		any_scope_state = {
			OR = {
				region = sr:region_north_germany
				region = sr:region_south_germany
			}
			is_incorporated = yes
			has_building = building_railway
			count >= 6
		}
	}

	prosperity_modifier = {
		military_formation_movement_speed_mult = 0.1
	}

	ai_weight = {
		value = 3 # Higher base value for flavored companies
	}
}

company_gwr = {

			}
		}
	}			
	
	possible = {
		any_scope_state = {
			state_region = s:STATE_WEST_COUNTRY

			state_region = s:STATE_MIDLANDS
			is_incorporated = yes
			has_building = building_railway
		}
		any_scope_state = {
			state_region = s:STATE_WALES

			has_building = building_railway
		}

			state_region = s:STATE_HOME_COUNTIES

		}
	}

		state_radicals_from_sol_change_mult = -0.05
	}	
	
	ai_weight = {
		value = 3 # Higher base value for flavored companies
	}
}

		hidden_trigger = { # Hide attainable if it's always fulfilled by possible
			any_scope_state = {
				OR = {
					state_region = s:STATE_ZULIA
					state_region = s:STATE_MIRANDA
				}
			}
		}
	}	
	
	possible = {
		any_scope_state = {
			OR = {
				state_region = s:STATE_ZULIA
				state_region = s:STATE_MIRANDA
			}
			is_incorporated = yes
			any_scope_building = {
				is_building_type = building_oil_rig
				level >= 5
			}
		}
		has_technology_researched = pumpjacks
	}
	
	prosperity_modifier = {
		country_convoys_capacity_mult = 0.1
		interest_group_ig_industrialists_approval_add = 3
	}
	
	ai_weight = {
		value = 3 # Higher base value for flavored companies
	}
}

	}

				state_region = s:STATE_CATALONIA

	}

			any_scope_building = {
				is_building_type = building_textile_mills
				level >= 3
			}

				}
				level >= 3
			}
		}

	}

		building_railway_throughput_add = 0.1
		interest_group_ig_industrialists_approval_add = 2
	}

	flavored_company = yes
	
	building_types = {  
		building_oil_rig
		building_railway
	}
	
	potential = {
		has_interest_marker_in_region = region_the_midwest
	}
	
	attainable = {
		hidden_trigger = { # Hide attainable if it's always fulfilled by possible
			any_scope_state = {
				region = sr:region_the_midwest
			}
		}
	}		
	
	possible = { 
		any_scope_state = {
			region = sr:region_the_midwest
			is_incorporated = yes
			any_scope_building = {
				is_building_type = building_oil_rig
				level >= 5
			}
		}
		has_technology_researched = pumpjacks
	}
	
	prosperity_modifier = {
		building_railway_throughput_add = 0.2
	}
	
	ai_weight = {
		value = 3 # Higher base value for flavored companies
	}
}

company_united_fruit = {
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/company_icons/historical_company_icons/american_united_fruit_co.dds"
	background = "gfx/interface/icons/company_icons/company_backgrounds/comp_illu_plantation.dds"
	
	flavored_company = yes
	
	building_types = {  
		building_banana_plantation
		building_sugar_plantation
	}	
	
	potential = {
		OR = {
			country_has_primary_culture = cu:yankee
			country_has_primary_culture = cu:dixie
		}
	}
	
	possible = {
		OR = {
			any_scope_state = {
				OR = {
					state_is_in_south_america = yes
					state_is_in_central_america = yes
				}
				any_scope_building = {
					is_building_type = building_banana_plantation
					level >= 5
				}
			}
		}
		any_subject_or_below = {
			OR = {
				country_is_in_south_america = yes
				country_is_in_central_america = yes
			}
			any_scope_state = {
				any_scope_building = {
					is_building_type = building_banana_plantation
					level >= 5
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	prosperity_modifier = {
		building_group_bg_plantations_throughput_add = 0.2
		country_infamy_decay_mult = -0.25
	}	
	
	ai_weight = {
		value = 3 # Higher base value for flavored companies
	}
}
